I locked onto Pullman because I discovered Panda Piggy Ranch while navigating on the map, which is about 15 minutes away by taxi from the hotel. By the way, taking a taxi from Jinhua is really cheap. It only costs about 12 yuan from the high-speed rail station to the hotel and from the hotel to the ranch. The two adults and one child chose the parent-child room. The room layout is reasonable and they are quite satisfied with the bathroom design. The toilet is naturally hidden in a corner. The towels and bath towels are large and thick, and the quality is better than that of Marriott. The wardrobe luggage space is also large, and the sliding doors move smoothly. The parent-child room comes with many children's toys, children's desks, chairs and books. What's shocking is that there is also a claw machine where you can practice empty grabbing. The layout of the room is too fancy, the background of the bedside is ocean style, and starry sky lights are hung on the roof. The room service must be praised. The elder sister is very kind and attentive to tidying up the room and adding supplies. The doorman's service attitude is also very good. Ctrip has the best booking price, but I cannot enjoy the rights of Accor Platinum members when I check in. Even if I propose to use the room upgrade coupon, I cannot enjoy the administrative benefits. The hotel's breakfast has plenty of carbohydrates, and several Jinhua specialty cakes are good. The millet porridge was very thin on the first day, but super thick on the second day. The cooking quality was too different. Letâ€™s talk about the deduction items. Hygiene is because there are a lot of mold spots on the tiles in the shower room. Facilities are because there is no USB interface in the room. Fortunately, I brought three power banks. The glass door of the shower room is not tightly sealed. Every time After taking a shower, there is a large puddle of water outside. The service level of the restaurant is not high, especially the noodle stall. The elder sister and a girl wearing glasses are both looking at their mobile phones. The hand that clicks on the mobile phone directly pulls the noodles. Even if there are customers ordering noodles and waiting for the noodles to be cooked, the two of them are still keen to watch. cell phone.
